< review>
Ok, let me start by saying that i am a pain in the **s kind of customer.  I shop and look and test drive and shop and shop, and i am always afraid of paying too much.  i also don't like bike dealers sales staff in general as these guys just do not listen.

These guys are quick, painless, professional, honest, and even friendly!  Rick took the lead as i was internet lead, and answered every question i asked and he knew the programs off the top of his head (one dealer i went to didn't even know they had low interest finance or that extras were included in the sale from the manufacturer!)  Every time i sent an email i got one back no matter how little the question was. No one ever told me they would need me to set up a "VIP Appointment" to get the best deal!!!!  lol!!!

Pricing?  They won't get beat, but to be honest, they had great pricing out of the gate, and no need to haggle.   Very fair!  Better than fair probably.

After the sale i wanted to add accessories, and without having to ask i was offered a discount on anything i wanted!   Andy in PARTS was great. A little place that's bigger inside than you may think.

What can i say?  I wish i lived closer because the Service dept has a great rep as well.  I may even take a trip for service, just because if they do that half as well as the sales end i'll be happy!

Great place to do business.  Highly recommend!</review>

<gmap_id>0x80e8291e4f851455:0xe00b4bcfdbb69d73<//gmap_id>< Review>
SVC is by far the worst motorcycle dealer in Ventura County, if not all of Southern California.  Their parts department does not carry a large inventory insuring that their customers will have to wait.  Their service department is staffed by young, untrained technicians who perform shoddy work.

I purchased a motorcycle from them in 2001.  Two years later it developed an intermittent missing problem and I brought it to them under warranty.  They tried on three separate occasions to find and repair the problem and couldn't.  They ended up giving the bike back to me un-repaired.  I then brought the bike to a competing dealer who diagnosed and located the problem in 10 minutes, ordered the part and returned my motorcycle in three days.

While SVC had my motorcycle the last time under warranty, they kept it for 4 weeks, broke my carburetor float bowls, glued them back together with epoxy, replaced defective parts with used ones, stored it outside in the rain (customary for them) and they returned the motorcycle to me completely filthy and corroded.  They refused to repair the damage they had caused or even detail the bike.

I highly recommend that you avoid Simi Valley Cycles.<//Review>

It was a disaster from the moment we stepped foot in the restaurant. Hostess desk staff were disorganized and running around like chickens with their heads cut off. Other patrons were grumbling about how disorganized they were as well.

We were sat upstairs among a field of ten tables surrounded by hotel rooms. We were greeted 15 minutes later as we were standing up to leave since our appeared that nobody was working that section despite full tables all around. Our overworked and under resourced waiter finally appeared and apologized and I asked him if the restaurant had anyone else working this section. Indeed, he was working alone. Despite that he was cheerful and tried his best to keep up with this massive section. This is beyond unsustainable.

The hotel guests kept walking through the tables and one group were screaming profanities and having a little party in their room. Very different energy than the outdoor dining experience we were hoping for. Also- no music playing at all.

The menu was what you would expect from an Asian fusion restaurant and the bar had some cute drinks that after a long wait finally arrived.

The food took forever and was both greasy and kinda bland for the type of cuisine it was.

No surprise to anyone, it took forever to get our bill and process payment.

Million dollar question: Why have servers at all if the restaurant won‚Äôt support them? Use technology for guests to order and pay online and have expediters run the food. Have a manager check in on how folks are doing. Have bussers offer clean up and refills. Other restaurants are doing this and it‚Äôs a better guest experience. Their current model is a huge fail.

< text>
Yikes. Disorganized & disinterested staff. For being a Asian Fusion restaurant, the complete lack of authentic flavors was a surprise.  We ordered dumplings to start and rice and noodles. The dumplings were a Monet- presented nice but a mess. All cheap peanuts and wrong mouthfeel.

We looked around and the only other people that looked like us were wiping tables. After an hour of waiting for basic rice and noodles, you look at everyone around you eating and enjoying themselves and it felt weird. It was like we in a parallel restaurant. This was my 1st time here and I won't be returning nor recommending to anyone.

We left without our dinner being served after an hours wait. The drinks - 2 beers, one in a can, came out to $30.

Save yourself the warm dining room and cold servers, take yourself to Bevmo for a Japanese beer and Panda Express afterwards.<//text>

< Text>
The bucks stops at the food... While the food taste great the service is abysmal at best. My partner and I have been to Roly several times (at least 6) and each time we mention Roly it's a struggle, we want the good food but dread the service/experience. I see allot of comments about the price. In all honesty I would happily pay these prices any day if the service were to match. The owners went to great lengths to design and lay out the concept but the service doesn't match that. When you pay $28 for white rice, brocolli and some beef I'd hope the service and experience were comparable for that price point. What bothers me the most is they always rush their patrons, I have never been able to have more than 1 or 2 cocktails with my dinner here. Generally my partner and I enjoy about 4 cocktails each with our meal. We also generally consume 2x bottles of still water. We've never been able to finish a bottle of water with our dinner. It's a shame that as much as we want out dollar to go to this establishment it feels as tho they don't want it. Sad to say but we won't be going back.<//Text>

< text>
This restaurant is owned by the same owners as Veit Fusion 533. I love 533. It's one of my favorite restaurants.  I was excited when I learned they were opening a Chinese restaurant. I've been to Roly three times. I have been 2x for lunch and once for dinner and i have thoroughly unimpressed. To me, it's an expensive Panda Express.  Roy's king pao chicken, good. But, not impressive in the slightest and very on par with Panda's. I tried their kimchee fried rice with lobster,  good. There was plenty of lobster,  but the fried rice wasn't anything special.  I'm not sure what the kimchee part was...maybe the onions were fermented (kimchee is a fermented coleslaw).  To me, this was just a mediocre fried rice with lobster.  Their prices for their dim sum...wow! EXPENSIVE!  Their dim sum is expensive like high end places in San Francisco or Vancouver and again,  good, but not special.  I love 533 and will continue enjoying them. I won't go back to Roly.< /text>

I'm tired of hearing about pizza. Pizza, Pizza, Pizza! Let's talk about Italian foods! Yes, I'm talking about Santino's Restaurant in Sherman Oaks. I'm talking about 5 stars 5 diamond food and get in and out for $20 bucks. There is no valet. Yes, there is free parking in the back and on the street! There are no waiters or waitresses. Yes, that means no double the tax for a tip! I just leave a buck or two in the jar at the counter.

Everyone that eats at the restaurant orders and pays for the food at the counter. Then the clerk or manager brings you the food at the table. Yes, there is inside dining or outside tables on the sidewalk! Nice!

<rate>5< /rate>< Text>
Easily the best pizza I've ever had. Was up in Los Angeles for the day with my dad, and we were in the area and hungry, just googled "pizza" and this place pops up. My dad is pickier than I am with pizza, but he thought we could try it. Right away when we got there, it was apparent this was genuine pizza. It's a little hole in the wall place, but the pizza was fantastic; thin crust, great sauce, awesome cheese and pepperoni. We're all the way from San Diego and this pizza was so good, we got another one to take home. Also, the owner, Daniel, is super friendly and nice. Will definitely be back if and when we're in the area!< /Text>

<user>114284842478595569607<//user><Text>I decided to have the motor rebuilt in my boat after an awful boating season a year and a half ago; chasing problem after problem. Eventually, I found the entire head for cylinders 2,4,6,8 had little compression. Not knowing exactly where to go, I did some shopping and eventually came across Paul at Rezurxn Speed and Marine. I spoke with Paul several times over the phone and met with him in person before deciding to have him rebuild my motor. First and foremost, I want to thank Paul for turning my boating season around last year. My family and I had an opportunity to use something we love to do dearly without having any major problems and am confident we will continued to do so as the years come and go.

I want to begin by explaining what I had built. A one sentence review does no one any good. I went from a factory 454 Mercruiser motor that was poorly re-built by the person who owned the boat before me. Once progress started, I had to remain optimistic and patient because I wanted it built correctly the first time. There was no short cuts and attention to detail was paramount for my wife and I. Once the engine was pulled, Paul remained in contact with me and updated me each step of the way. I was hopeful to reuse some parts of the motor to cut down cost; however, as the engine was disassembled, Paul found several crucial components were damaged beyond re-use. This was at the fault of a poor engine builder. The parts were saved and Paul was able to show them to me and explained why they were damaged. Looking at each part, it was obviously damaged and I would have been foolish to re-use the parts. At no point did I feel he was trying to get into my wallet. They were broken parts plain and simple. Parts that cannot be seen from looking at the outside of a motor. Paul was able to give me options on what to do which included cheaper parts and more expensive performance parts. Paul explained to me the pros and cons of each as well as providing his input on what he would do if it was his. I listened to his recommendations some of which were in my favor for lower cost.

This engine build grew into quite the project, I didn't have a crystal ball to look into. Turns out who ever machined the engine, did it wrong and machined each side of the engine to two different cylinder bore sizes and put smaller pistons in the even side. Paul was able to determine the rings of the piston didn't even touch and was the cause for the poor compression. I explain this because several things have to happen at the point, machine work, nitrating a crank, matching a cam shaft, carburation, intake size,  the list is just about endless. At this point, I decided to BUILD a motor, If I have to replace major parts I might as well make it generate more horse power. All aluminum heads, valves, springs, pushrods, etc. were replaced with performance parts. That kind of prep work takes time.

Once reassembly began, Paul remained in contact with me; keeping me updated each step of the way. After paint and powder coat was finished, the engine was fully reassembled and placed onto a break in stand. I had the opportunity to push the button at Paul's shop to start my motor for the first time and listen to it before it went back into my boat.

I take great pride in the things I own and Paul is the same way. He and his guys at the shop treated my boat as if it was their own. Again, attention to detail is paramount and it shows. I must say good work takes time. This project didn't happen over night, it didn't even happen in a month, but its important that you understand when you have something custom built, that means its one of a kind. There is no other motor that looks, sounds, drives like mine. This isn't an engine that's getting built by the 1000's on an assembly line somewhere.

I have since been back to Rezurxn Speed and Marine to have my boat stereo installed and soon to have a sub enclosure built for my mustang. I most definitely recommend this location to anyone and will continue to go there myself for any of my performance needs.<//Text><name>jeff holcombe< /name><gmap_id>0x80c3674f86f67e3f:0x35bf2c169f468da9</gmap_id></record>

< Text>
When sales people come to visit at work they tend to bring Lady Di's cookies - it is such a happy treat for the lab! Finally got the chance to visit the place myself... and it did not disappoint.

Location wise - not hard to find and along the old road. Small store, not much but a display and cashier. Parking was fine it's a big plaza so there's bound to be a spot for you.

Service was friendly and quick... they had tons of options and it was already 4 in the afternoon...

I needed some dessert for my GodMothers birthday - didn't think I needed that many so I got 1/2 a dozen of cupcakes and 1/2 dozen cookies. cookies here are delicious! Oreo crave is my go to but my absolute favorite has to be the oatmeal chocolate chip. Their cookies are $1.50 each but they're pretty big so the price makes sense. Their cupcakes were delicious as well and their were some fun flavors I definitely had to try... banana cream pie was good. Wasn't too sweet so I enjoyed it a lot. They had a blueberry lemon and I thought it was pretty good... I didn't think their cupcakes were overwhelming, so they were a perfect purchase for a group of older folk not looking for some something TOO sweet. They were $3 per cupcake which is pretty standard at a shop like this.

Didn't mind the price and would come back here again.<//Text>

I reported the concern to the guy working, and he came back with paper napkin and gave slight cosmetic brush up. The stickiness / gum stayed and I needed a power outlet. I moved to other end of couch and stopped using the table.

While cleanliness is one of the reasons for low rating, below is more concerning.

Lack of customer friendly attitude: While Respect/manners is common among most educated groups, these folks come short with these. When you request for something, their eyes and body language resemble a teenager who was bored of cleaning his/her room when asked by parents.

< text>
I have lived down the street from this restaurant for so many years and for all that time I never thought about visiting this restaurant. When I did, I regret the wasted years that I could have been enjoying the delicious food that is prepared and served. While the seating is limited this place is a great place to stop by for lunch or to pick up and take for dinner. Their menu is varied and has things from breakfast to tacos, quesadillas, burritos, tortas and even fried food. They have plenty of combination plates or you order each item individually. They also boast a weekend special of Birria or Menudo for 8.99 only Saturdays and Sundays. This place is always a go to for me and is the place I recommend to everyone who is looking for a great taco or burrito. If given the chance go try this place I say go, and enjoy the delicious food.<//text>

< Review>
This is an honest review.
My car was rear-ended and the driver who hit me had Geico insurance. They recommended Carlsbad Collision Center for the repairs, so I just went with them hoping there would be no fuss. Geico were actually really good about getting my car in within 5 days of the accident.
Things started to go awry after I had checked my car in. A few days later I called to see what the status was. It took 3 calls over the course of 2 days for someone to call me back, which caused frustration on my part. It was explained to me that the part needed was on back order and would take 10 days or so to get in, which was fine with me as I had a paid rental car.
After 11 or 12 days they called me to say my car was ready, so I went to pick it up. Signed the documents to release my car and was given the keys, but on inspection I realized the work done was not up to par. Firstly the color of the replaced bumper didn't match. Also the masking job they did on the paint was very 2nd rate. Wavy lines and over-spray. There were also green pen marks on the replaced bumper. To top it off they had parked my car under a sappy tree and it was totally filthy.
The adjuster recognized that the job done was not up to standard and promised I'd have my car fixed (again) back to OEM in a day or so.
I called 2 days later and was told my car was ready for pickup. I asked for it to be washed, and for the work to be double checked.
This 2nd time my car was perfect and clean, inside and out.
I'm glad to get my car back but the work carried out here (just a rear bumper and related attachments) should have been perfect first time.
They were apologetic, but that's not the point.
Please watch the quality control if u must have work done here.
For sure I will never return.< /Review>

Check out line: May the force be with you. Patience, friends.

Will I go back: Only if I am in that area.</text>

<text>A really good Target. I do wish the clothing offered by the usual brands (Mossimo in particular) had more consistent measurements, size-wise.
I have a pair of year-old jeans, size 3L, that are very form-fitting. Almost tight after a wash. They are also very, very short in length. The same can be said of a pair of much older Mossimo jeans, which are 4R's, though they are a bit less tight, and a bit longer.

I bought several pairs of jeans more recently, and I was shocked to find myself barely able to keep them from falling off. Two pairs are size 0 and 0L, and both are also so long that the regular length is okay when cuffed, but the longer length stubbornly refuses to stop covering my shoes, so that I end up walking on them.  The third pair of jeans were actually boyfriend-style jeggings, and after I exchanged them twice, I wound up with a pair of 0's, and I have shrunk them twice, so that i can finally keep them up without using my hands, but they are unbelievably loose. No need for that "power stretch," ladies; at least, not anymore.

Still, this store has decent selection, and the additional hour they are open is always great... If you miss another Target's hours, you can always run up to this store and grab a quick thing or two.  The staff is friendly, and the location is extremely convenient.< /text></record></dataset><record>

<Text>I went into the Emeryville Target today to discover that the store only accepts 1 like manufacture coupon and 1 target coupon per transaction.  This was very disappointing as their store policy states the following:
Only one manufacturer coupon (paper or Cartwheel digital), one Target coupon (paper or digital), and one Cartwheel‚Ñ† offer can be combined per item (unless otherwise noted on coupon).
We have the right to refuse, or limit the use of any coupon and/or the subsequent return for any reason, including if guests' reoccurring behavior becomes disruptive or the items are deemed not to be for the purpose of using or gifting.
Limit of 4 identical coupons per household, per day (unless otherwise noted on coupon).  I was trying to purchase 3 tide pod products, nothing out of the ordinary.  So why the need to refuse the coupons?  I don't know why anyone would ever want to shop at this store? I explained to the CSM that their policy states otherwise and she proceeded to tell me how they have the right to refuse the coupons period!

The whole experience was unpleasant.   When we first stepped up to the cash register the cashier was on her cell phone speaking to someone very loudly.  She was obviously on a personal call. < text>
If you live in Berkeley, you basically have two choices for Target: Emeryville or El Cerrito. Yes, there is a tiny target near UC campus, but it is impossible to park there and the selection is highly limited.

The Emeryville store is as good a Target as any, but it does seem like the staff is more friendly than any other Target store I have been to in the Bay Area.  The cashiers are usually smiling and warm, so the hiring manager at this store must be pretty good.

The store is big with just one floor compared to the (I think) slightly smaller Target in El Cerrito that has two floors. I prefer the single floor layout.

The downside to this Target is that it gets really, really busy. The El Cerrito store is not as busy, so I go to one Target or the other, depending on the time of day. El Cerrito is better during any busy time, like after work or on weekends.  The Emeryville store is better in the morning before 12 noon on weekdays.<//text>
